    @ $mol_mem
    formatter() {
      return new Intl.NumberFormat()
    }

    override mask(val: string) {
      if (! val) return ''
      const current = Number(val.replace(/[^\d\.\-]/g, ''))
      if (Number.isNaN(current)) return ''
      return this.formatter().format(current).replace(/[^\s]/g, '_')
    }
